double \textbf{ get\+Actual\+Radius} (int v)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Return actual radius of a vertex, meaning in the hyp case the "{}x-\/radius"{} is converted to the actual hyperbolic radius, which is what outside world should see. In hyp case, when x-\/radius$<$0, it is -\/r for eucl radius r, so we just return -\/r. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
double \textbf{ get\+Radius} (int v)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Return the stored radius; if v is a red vertex, this may be stored in a red edge. In the hyp case, return the x-\/radius. (See \textquotesingle{}get\+Actual\+Radius\textquotesingle{} to instead convert x-\/radius to actual hyp radius.). \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
void \textbf{ set\+Radius\+Actual} (int v, double r)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Store given radius \textquotesingle{}r\textquotesingle{} in internal form. Only issue is hyp case:\+ when r$>$8.\+0, treat as horocycle, when \textquotesingle{}r\textquotesingle{} is the actual hyperbolic radius, it is converted to x\+\_\+radius for storage. ~\newline
 For numerical reasons, small hyp radii \textquotesingle{}r\textquotesingle{} is converted to x=2$\ast$r$\ast$(2-\/r$\ast$(1-\/2$\ast$r/\+3)). (Recall x=1-\/exp(-\/2h)=1-\/s$^\wedge$2.). \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
void \textbf{ set\+Radius} (int v, double r)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Store radius for \textquotesingle{}v\textquotesingle{} (in all its locations). (\textquotesingle{}r\textquotesingle{} is in internal form; i.\+e., in hyp case, \textquotesingle{}r\textquotesingle{} should already be in x\+\_\+radius form. If it needs to be converted, call \textquotesingle{}set\+Radius\+Actual\textquotesingle{}.) e.\+g., in \textquotesingle{}\doxyref{Red\+Edge}{p.}{classcombinatorics_1_1komplex_1_1_red_edge}\textquotesingle{}s.). \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em If w is neighbor of v, return its index in the flower of v; else return -\/1. Note this works for DCEL structures, but answer is no so useful if not -\/1. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\textbf{ Complex}[$\,$] \textbf{ corners\+\_\+dual\+\_\+face} (int v)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Return non-\/closed list of corners for dual face for v, mainly centers of faces. For bdry v, add the partial edges ending at the tang pts of the two bdry edges. For v red, assume initial face is in place, but the proceed face-\/by-\/face. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
\textbf{ Complex}[$\,$] \textbf{ vertex\+\_\+hull} (int v)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Return non-\/closed list of corners hull of v, formed by the tangency points of edges from v, including v itself if v is bdry. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
\textbf{ Complex}[$\,$] \textbf{ face\+\_\+hull} (\textbf{ combinatorics.\+komplex.\+Dcel\+Face} face)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Return corners of "{}hull"{} for this face; that is, formed by the tangency points of the face edges. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
\textbf{ Complex}[$\,$] \textbf{ corners\+\_\+face} (int f)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Return non-\/closed list of corners for face f, in correct order. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
\textbf{ Complex}[$\,$] \textbf{ corners\+\_\+paver} (int v)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Return non-\/closed list of corners for "{}paver"{} of v, i.\+e., polygonal region defined as union of v\textquotesingle{}s faces (include center of v itself if bdry). If v is red, we treat its first face as in place, but successively recompute the remaining faces based on radii. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
\textbf{ Complex}[$\,$] \textbf{ ends\+\_\+dual\+\_\+edge} (\textbf{ Edge\+Simple} edge)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Return complex locations of ends of dual edge $<$f,g$>$. If the edge between is red, we do a faux layout of g to get its incircle. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
int[$\,$] \textbf{ flower\+Fan} (int v, int j1, int j2)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em return the fan of petal vertices from index j1 to and including j2. Null on error or if v is bdry and j1$>$=j2. If v is interior, treat j1, j2 mod num, and if j1==j2, return full flower, but starting/\+ending with j1. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\item 
double \textbf{ comp\+\_\+inv\+\_\+dist} (int v, int w)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Return inversive distance between circles for v and w, not necessarily neighbors. Inv\+Dist rho goes from -\/1 to infinity. rho is in [-\/1,1] for overlap situation, then rho=cos(overlap angle); rho=0 for orthogonal circles; rho=1 for tangency; rho$>$1 for separated circles, where inv\+Dist is cosh of the hyperbolic distance between the circles (bubbled into hyperbolic upper half space). \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
double \textbf{ xyz\+\_\+inv\+\_\+dist} (\textbf{ Point3D} xyz, \textbf{ Point3D} XYZ, double r, double R)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Find overlap/\+inversive distance between euclidean spheres of given 3-\/space centers/\+radii. Return 1 (tangency) on error. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
int \textbf{ fillcurves} ()
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Fill in the angle sums (curvature) of the packing. Note that angle sums at a vertex are computed face-\/by-\/face for faces containing that vertex. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
boolean \textbf{ s\+\_\+anglesum} (int v, double r, \textbf{ Util\+Packet} uP)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Find anglesum at given vertex. Inversive distances not yet included. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
boolean \textbf{ h\+\_\+anglesum\+\_\+overlap} (int v, double x, \textbf{ Util\+Packet} uP)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Compute anglesum in hyperbolic geometry. Result in u\+P.\+value. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
boolean \textbf{ h\+\_\+radcalc} (int v, double r, double aim, int N, \textbf{ Util\+Packet} uP)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Computes radius at vert v that gives anglesum closer to aim; use secant method, r = first guess, N is a limit on the number of iterations. New radius will not increase or decrease beyond what \textquotesingle{}factor\textquotesingle{} allows. (Thus, may need repeated calls to this routine.) Return true if everything seems okay. Calling routine responsible for actually changing the radius of v, given u\+P.\+value. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
boolean \textbf{ e\+\_\+radcalc} (int v, double r, double aim, int N, \textbf{ Util\+Packet} uP)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Computes radius at vert v that gives anglesum closer to aim; use secant method, r = first guess, N is a limit on the number of iterations. New radius is returned in u\+P.\+value, but will not increase or decrease beyond what \textquotesingle{}factor\textquotesingle{} allows. (Thus, may need repeated calls to this routine.) int \textbf{ right\+\_\+slide} (\textbf{ Half\+Link} hlink)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em This is more general version of \textquotesingle{}hex\+\_\+slide\textquotesingle{} mechanism. Perform an edge flip on the edge to the right of each halfedge in \textquotesingle{}hlink\textquotesingle{}, i.\+e., flip twin.\+next. The effect when \textquotesingle{}hlink\textquotesingle{} is closed half-\/hex loop is to cut the packing along hlink and slide the right side one notch down before reattaching. int \textbf{ data\+Put\+Get} (\textbf{ Pack\+Data} q, Vector$<$ Vector$<$ String $>$ $>$ flagsegs, boolean putget, boolean transl)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Does the work for the "{}get\+\_\+data"{} and "{}put\+\_\+data"{} calls, depending on \textquotesingle{}putget\textquotesingle{} flag. If \textquotesingle{}put\textquotesingle{}, then data goes from \textquotesingle{}this\textquotesingle{} to \textquotesingle{}q\textquotesingle{}; \textquotesingle{}get\textquotesingle{} goes from \textquotesingle{}q\textquotesingle{} to \textquotesingle{}this\textquotesingle{}. Caution:\+ \textquotesingle{}translate\textquotesingle{} true means the \textquotesingle{}\doxyref{Vertex\+Map}{p.}{classlist_manip_1_1_vertex_map}\textquotesingle{} of \textquotesingle{}this\textquotesingle{} is used to associate source with target. So use of \textquotesingle{}put\textquotesingle{}/\+\textquotesingle{}get\textquotesingle{} with translation depends on who has the appropriate \textquotesingle{}\doxyref{Vertex\+Map}{p.}{classlist_manip_1_1_vertex_map}\textquotesingle{}. TODO:\+ multiple translations? we currently only use the first. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\item 
int \textbf{ hex\+Cell} (int v, int w, int n, \textbf{ Node\+Link} vert\+Chain)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Try to draw a combinatorial hexagon of side length n, starting at corner v, in direction of neighbor w. Pretend combinatorics are hex:\+ do 6 n-\/step edges, and left turns. Fill \textquotesingle{}vert\+Chain\textquotesingle{} with indices. Return length on success, -\/length if an edge or other combinatoric problem (eg, not enough edges from a vertex) is encountered. Success means completing the walk, but that does not necessarily mean a return to v. (I think the "{}\+Berger\textquotesingle{}s"{} vector of physics is the displacement from the center of v to the center of the end vertex.). \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em When clicking on circle in this packing, display it for this canvas and also display the associated circle in the q canvas. Translate directly if \textquotesingle{}this.\+node\+Count\textquotesingle{} and \textquotesingle{}q.\+node\+Count\textquotesingle{} are equal or if \textquotesingle{}this.\+vertex\+Map\textquotesingle{} doesn\textquotesingle{}t exist. Else, translate using \textquotesingle{}this.\+vertex\+Map\textquotesingle{}. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

int \textbf{ match} (\textbf{ Pack\+Data} qack\+Data, int v1, int v2, int w1, int w2, \textbf{ Mobius} mob)

static \textbf{ Mobius} \textbf{ holonomy\+Mobius} (\textbf{ Pack\+Data} p, \textbf{ Half\+Link} hlink)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Compute \doxyref{Mobius}{p.}{classmath_1_1_mobius} associated with holonomy along a closed chain of faces. The faces are defined by given \textquotesingle{}\doxyref{Half\+Link}{p.}{classlist_manip_1_1_half_link}\textquotesingle{}, the first assumed to be in the desired geometric location. Centers are then recomputed iteratively until the final locations of the original face vertices are found. Note that data in the packing is not changed. The transformation and its Frobenius norm (how close to identity) are displayed in \textquotesingle{}Messages\textquotesingle{} and written to a file if fp!=null. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
static \textbf{ Pack\+Data} \textbf{ sch\+Flower\+Err} (\textbf{ Vertex} vert, \textbf{ Complex} err, \textbf{ Circle\+Simple} cs)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Generate a euclidean flower packing based on \textquotesingle{}vert\textquotesingle{} but using only its intrinsic schwarzians and recover the \textquotesingle{}error\textquotesingle{} in layout of the last petal. See \textquotesingle{}\doxyref{Pack\+Creation.\+seed}{p.}{classpacking_1_1_pack_creation_af1bd24fca1666865ca8d25f9d01a72d6}\textquotesingle{} for description. Comparing initial/\+final layouts of cn lead to the \textquotesingle{}err\textquotesingle{}=x+iy, where:\+ x = (newrad -\/ rad)/\+rad for cn y = (anglechange -\/ aim)/\+aim \textquotesingle{}cs\textquotesingle{} contains the new data for cn in case the user wants to use it. \end{DoxyCompactList}\end{DoxyCompactItemize}

\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
The fundamental data repository for a circle packing in \doxyref{Circle\+Pack}{p.}{classall_mains_1_1_circle_pack}. 

This is the fundamental data repository for a circle packing and is associated with a CPDrawing for display. This is a workhorse, with methods for reading/\+writing, combinatorics, and manipulations. \begin{DoxyAuthor}{Author}
kens, sometime last century 
\end{DoxyAuthor}

Definition at line \textbf{ 3181} of file \textbf{ Pack\+Data.\+java}.

\index{packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}!adjacency@{adjacency}}
\index{adjacency@{adjacency}!packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}}
\doxysubsubsection{adjacency()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpacking_1_1_pack_data_a73282779bd43b17cc70a8a7af848eeb1} 
int packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+adjacency (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Buffered\+Writer}]{fp}{, }\item[{boolean}]{tm}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Save adjacency matrix of packing ($<$= 10,000 verts) in form for matlab to read; the adjacency matrix has a 1 in (i,j) spot if i and j are neighboring vertices, else a 0.

If \textquotesingle{}tm\textquotesingle{} is true, divide every row by sum of its entries and set the rows for boundary vertices to zero:\+ this yields the "{}transition"{} matrix for the "{}simple"{} (ie. equal probability) random walk on the edge-\/graph of the packing with absorbing boundary. Also add an ordered list of the boundary vertices to the matlab file. Return 0 on error.

\doxysubsubsection{antipodal\_verts()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpacking_1_1_pack_data_a1018bffccaf14b13f1400ec889700060} 
\textbf{ Node\+Link} packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+antipodal\+\_\+verts (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Node\+Link}}]{ants}{, }\item[{int}]{N}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Return N successive "{}antipodal"{} vertices, starting with given list \textquotesingle{}ants\textquotesingle{}. That is, having reached list \{v1, v2, ..., vj\}, inductively the next so it is the furthest combinatorial distance from predecessors until we have N in the list. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ants} & \doxyref{Node\+Link}{p.}{classlist_manip_1_1_node_link}; if empty, start with max vert index. \\
\hline
{\em N} & int, number we want in list, (including \textquotesingle{}ants\textquotesingle{}) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxyref{Node\+Link}{p.}{classlist_manip_1_1_node_link}, v1,...,vN; null on error. NOTE:\+ if \textquotesingle{}ants\textquotesingle{} has N or more elements, return these. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpacking_1_1_pack_data_a84697da6c316971aa90dc56121d1eaa0} 
int packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+apply\+\_\+\+Mobius (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Mobius}}]{Mob}{, }\item[{\textbf{ Node\+Link}}]{vertlist}{, }\item[{boolean}]{oriented}{, }\item[{boolean}]{sp\+\_\+flag}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Apply \doxyref{Mobius}{p.}{classmath_1_1_mobius} Mob (oriented) or inverse to specified list of circles in all occurrences; if sp\+\_\+flag is true (default), also recompute the side-\/pairing maps. For hyperbolic ideal circles, also adjust the negative radius (which reflects euclidean radius of horocycle). (Note, if Mob is one of the side-\/pairing maps, then application will simply permute the others, so sp\+\_\+flag is turned off, eg., when applying covering maps.).

\index{packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}!blend@{blend}}
\index{blend@{blend}!packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}}
\doxysubsubsection{blend()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpacking_1_1_pack_data_a32c8af26ed7d5a16425039bc147a03ab} 
int packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+blend (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Pack\+Data}}]{q}{, }\item[{int}]{bdry\+\_\+vert}{, }\item[{int}]{depth}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

"{}\+Blending"{} refers to the attachment of one packing to another, generally with some overlap where a smooth transition in radii and centers from one pack to the other can be made. (Eg., packing \textquotesingle{}islands\textquotesingle{} generated with Plug\+Pack or "{}mending"{} a flaw.)

Blend pack q centers/\+radii with pack p centers/\+radii, putting result in pack p. (Assume both p, q have been packed.) The vertex\+Map of q will be used to identify circles of q with the corresponding circles of p.

\textquotesingle{}bdry\+\_\+vert\textquotesingle{} is a bdry vert of q; it and its bdry antipital will be used for registration purposes, and the resulting mobius is applied to pack q. Presumably the packing combinatorics are such that they overlap in a certain combinatorial annulus; \textquotesingle{}depth\textquotesingle{} indicates how many generations (counting done in q) are used to smoothly blend the centers of p with those of q -- the closer to bdry q, the more heavily the centers of p are weighted. Depth 1 means just line up bdry\+\_\+vert and its antipital; depth $<$ 0 means allow largest possible depth.

Return number of generations blended (may be less than depth). Return 0 on error. 

Definition at line \textbf{ 6492} of file \textbf{ Pack\+Data.\+java}.

\index{packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}!color\_qc@{color\_qc}}
\index{color\_qc@{color\_qc}!packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}}
\doxysubsubsection{color\_qc()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpacking_1_1_pack_data_ae96339c289ea45642e787ba27c7127e3} 
int packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+color\+\_\+qc (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Vector$<$ Vector$<$ String $>$ $>$}]{flag\+Segs}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Color faces depending on quasiconformal dilatations. Options include the qc-\/dilatation for a mapping from p to q; because face data is ephemeral, we need p and q to have essentially the same combinatorics and same face indices (for instance, one can\textquotesingle{}t change alpha since that would reset face indices). Both p and q must be euclidean. 

Also can compare to eucl pack p to its stored xyz-\/coordinates or (eventually) to those in a file.

\index{packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}!color\_qc\_map@{color\_qc\_map}}
\index{color\_qc\_map@{color\_qc\_map}!packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}}
\doxysubsubsection{color\_qc\_map()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpacking_1_1_pack_data_a61d3bc0f3e4ba43ff921b39c7ca18433} 
double packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+color\+\_\+qc\+\_\+map (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Pack\+Data}}]{q}{, }\item[{double}]{maxdil}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Color faces to show quasiconformal dilatation for map from \textquotesingle{}this\textquotesingle{} to \textquotesingle{}q\textquotesingle{}. Non-\/eucl data converted to eucl for the computation (3D eucl flat triangles for sphere). Shades of red based on quasiconformal dilatation, blue for those beyond \textquotesingle{}maxdil\textquotesingle{}. (Note:\+ the faces should have corresponding triples of vertices, as when p and q are packings of the same complex, but we only check that the face indices are legal.).

\index{packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}!color\_qc\_xyz@{color\_qc\_xyz}}
\index{color\_qc\_xyz@{color\_qc\_xyz}!packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}}
\doxysubsubsection{color\_qc\_xyz()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpacking_1_1_pack_data_a7684cf90318f246d7857aa835e31d399} 
double packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+color\+\_\+qc\+\_\+xyz (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Point3D}[$\,$]}]{xyz\+\_\+list}{, }\item[{int}]{xyzcount}{, }\item[{double}]{maxdil}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



For map between 2 (eucl) packings, color faces of p in shades of red based on quasiconformal dilatation of the map. (Note:\+ the faces should have corresponding triples of vertices, as when p and q are packings of the same complex with same alpha, but we only check that the face indices are legal.). 

For each carrier face, we use the xyz location of the circle centers. If geom is hyp, use eucl centers, if sph, use xyz locations on unit sphere.

TODO:\+ This can be a problem is packing isn\textquotesingle{}t laying out coherently and you wanted to use stored radii/\+overlaps to compute edge lengths. Might put in a flag to cover this, but still have problems in hyp/\+sph cases.

TODO:\+ Should use correct geometry instead of converting to euclidean:\+ e.\+g., result is not \doxyref{Mobius}{p.}{classmath_1_1_mobius} invariant.

\index{packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}!comp\_inv\_dist@{comp\_inv\_dist}}
\index{comp\_inv\_dist@{comp\_inv\_dist}!packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}}
\doxysubsubsection{comp\_inv\_dist()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpacking_1_1_pack_data_a9eab993be20682216eab9816b36fe48c} 
double packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+comp\+\_\+inv\+\_\+dist (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{v}{, }\item[{int}]{w}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Return inversive distance between circles for v and w, not necessarily neighbors. Inv\+Dist rho goes from -\/1 to infinity. rho is in [-\/1,1] for overlap situation, then rho=cos(overlap angle); rho=0 for orthogonal circles; rho=1 for tangency; rho$>$1 for separated circles, where inv\+Dist is cosh of the hyperbolic distance between the circles (bubbled into hyperbolic upper half space). 

TODO:\+ routines not very robust

So use of \textquotesingle{}put\textquotesingle{}/\+\textquotesingle{}get\textquotesingle{} with translation depends on who has the appropriate \textquotesingle{}\doxyref{Vertex\+Map}{p.}{classlist_manip_1_1_vertex_map}\textquotesingle{}. {\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpacking_1_1_pack_data_ae802deddb726ee84e9656b98888185c1} 
boolean packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+e\+\_\+radcalc (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{v}{, }\item[{double}]{r}{, }\item[{double}]{aim}{, }\item[{int}]{N}{, }\item[{\textbf{ Util\+Packet}}]{uP}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Computes radius at vert v that gives anglesum closer to aim; use secant method, r = first guess, N is a limit on the number of iterations. New radius is returned in u\+P.\+value, but will not increase or decrease beyond what \textquotesingle{}factor\textquotesingle{} allows. (Thus, may need repeated calls to this routine.) Return true if everything seems okay. Calling routine responsible for actually changing the radius of v.

Definition at line \textbf{ 2221} of file \textbf{ Pack\+Data.\+java}.

\index{packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}!edge\_search@{edge\_search}}
\index{edge\_search@{edge\_search}!packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}}
\doxysubsubsection{edge\_search()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpacking_1_1_pack_data_ac45a070865b8b658cbd7404fc06c32b6} 
\textbf{ Edge\+Link} packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+edge\+\_\+search (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Complex}}]{z}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

TODO:\+ This is very iffy stuff; needs lots of refinement. Given complex number z, find the closest edge of the packing. Return null if no appropriate edge is found or if there is too much ambiguity. For now, can\textquotesingle{}t handle non-\/simply connected spherical cases. (And in general, could be flaky in spherical case where there are more ambiguities.)

The procedure differs for simply/\+multiply connected; in the former, we can look for a face containing z first and if not found, we search only for the closest bdry edge.

For multiply connected, faces may not have coherent layout. So we search for closest circle center, then search based on distances to edges from it. This can also fail, e.\+g., for ghost circles, circles on the red chain, etc. 

Definition at line \textbf{ 4456} of file \textbf{ Pack\+Data.\+java}.

\index{packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}!face\_dilatation@{face\_dilatation}}
\index{face\_dilatation@{face\_dilatation}!packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}}
\doxysubsubsection{face\_dilatation()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpacking_1_1_pack_data_aeff7eca051ea4160e6ad7191741a53ac} 
double packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+face\+\_\+dilatation (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Pack\+Data}}]{q}{, }\item[{int}]{face}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Compute the quasiconformal dilatation of map between faces in \textquotesingle{}this\textquotesingle{} packing and packing q. 

We use edge lengths so this can apply to triangulations independent of circles -- e.\+g. random Delaunay.

Treat centers as eucl (3D in sphere case). For hyperbolic, do NOT convert (that would require radii as well), just treat as euclidean. For sphere, use 3D edge lengths.

TODO:\+ we only do eucl computations so far.

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\index{packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}!flipable@{flipable}}
\index{flipable@{flipable}!packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}}
\doxysubsubsection{flipable()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpacking_1_1_pack_data_a07a221d505466f6549705eb1fd07a1fa} 
boolean packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+flipable (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{v}{, }\item[{int}]{w}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Determine if edge \{v,w\} is "{}flipable"{} (as in Whitehead move). Situations that fail:\+ 


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item if flip would result in vert of degree 2
\item if the new edge would connect two verts already neighbors (can happen, e.\+g., when one neighbor has degree three);
\item new edge will have both ends on boundary, could disconnect interior or isolate a bdry vert. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em v} & int \\
\hline
{\em w} & int \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
boolean 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxyItemize}

\index{packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}!flowerFan@{flowerFan}}
\index{flowerFan@{flowerFan}!packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}}
\doxysubsubsection{flowerFan()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpacking_1_1_pack_data_a0c1f73cafbb260e97fbb3ebf381ec8a1} 
int[$\,$] packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+flower\+Fan (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{v}{, }\item[{int}]{j1}{, }\item[{int}]{j2}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



return the fan of petal vertices from index j1 to and including j2. Null on error or if v is bdry and j1$>$=j2. If v is interior, treat j1, j2 mod num, and if j1==j2, return full flower, but starting/\+ending with j1. 

Note:\+ added 2/\+2015 for conformal tiling \textquotesingle{}feedback\textquotesingle{} code, but may be useful to improve other routines.

\index{gen\_mark@{gen\_mark}!packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}}
\doxysubsubsection{gen\_mark()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpacking_1_1_pack_data_aca83f4ce36af74680092130c59105786} 
int packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+gen\+\_\+mark (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Node\+Link}}]{seedlist}{, }\item[{int}]{mx}{, }\item[{boolean}]{mark}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Determine generation of vertices starting from given seeds. If \textquotesingle{}mark\textquotesingle{} is true, store in \textquotesingle{}\doxyref{Vertex.\+mark}{p.}{classcombinatorics_1_1komplex_1_1_vertex_ac0c420b48123de31127ad3c7b5392bef}\textquotesingle{}, else just return the index of the last vertex. \textquotesingle{}util\+Flag\textquotesingle{} is used to pass seed info to \textquotesingle{}label\+\_\+generations\textquotesingle{}. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mx} & int, if mx$>$0, stop at generation mx. \\
\hline
{\em seedlist} & \doxyref{Node\+Link}{p.}{classlist_manip_1_1_node_link}, list defined as first generation (1) \\
\hline
{\em mark} & boolean, if true, store as \textquotesingle{}mark in \textquotesingle{}\doxyref{Vertex}{p.}{classcombinatorics_1_1komplex_1_1_vertex}\textquotesingle{}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
int, index of last\+\_\+vert (first encountered in max generation), 0 on error 
\end{DoxyReturn}

int packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+geom\+\_\+to\+\_\+h (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Converts centers/\+radii to euclidean first, then scales packing to live in the unit disc and converts to hyp center and s-\/radii. Sets hes=-\/1. Note:\+ does NOT adjust \textquotesingle{}CPDrawing\textquotesingle{} geometry.

\end{DoxyReturn}

double packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+get\+Actual\+Radius (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{v}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Return actual radius of a vertex, meaning in the hyp case the "{}x-\/radius"{} is converted to the actual hyperbolic radius, which is what outside world should see. In hyp case, when x-\/radius$<$0, it is -\/r for eucl radius r, so we just return -\/r.

\index{packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}!h\_radcalc@{h\_radcalc}}
\index{h\_radcalc@{h\_radcalc}!packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}}
\doxysubsubsection{h\_radcalc()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpacking_1_1_pack_data_a4351099317f647df3e0d940a2ce1ea38} 
boolean packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+h\+\_\+radcalc (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{v}{, }\item[{double}]{r}{, }\item[{double}]{aim}{, }\item[{int}]{N}{, }\item[{\textbf{ Util\+Packet}}]{uP}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Computes radius at vert v that gives anglesum closer to aim; use secant method, r = first guess, N is a limit on the number of iterations. New radius will not increase or decrease beyond what \textquotesingle{}factor\textquotesingle{} allows. (Thus, may need repeated calls to this routine.) Return true if everything seems okay. Calling routine responsible for actually changing the radius of v, given u\+P.\+value.

\index{packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}!hex\_refine@{hex\_refine}}
\index{hex\_refine@{hex\_refine}!packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpacking_1_1_pack_data_a045d79ff8656e1fd3d70c2c8f7536fb1} 
int packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+hex\+\_\+refine (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

We are operating on this packing. Each edge gets new vertex, each face broken into 4 faces. Try to propagate old centers/\+radii, overlaps, schwarzians to new edges. Return 0 on failure. 

Definition at line \textbf{ 4800} of file \textbf{ Pack\+Data.\+java}.

\index{packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}!hexCell@{hexCell}}
\index{hexCell@{hexCell}!packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}}
\doxysubsubsection{hexCell()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpacking_1_1_pack_data_ac3c863fbafd479629e59d044aea87359} 
int packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+hex\+Cell (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{v}{, }\item[{int}]{w}{, }\item[{int}]{n}{, }\item[{\textbf{ Node\+Link}}]{vert\+Chain}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Try to draw a combinatorial hexagon of side length n, starting at corner v, in direction of neighbor w. Pretend combinatorics are hex:\+ do 6 n-\/step edges, and left turns. Fill \textquotesingle{}vert\+Chain\textquotesingle{} with indices. Return length on success, -\/length if an edge or other combinatoric problem (eg, not enough edges from a vertex) is encountered. Success means completing the walk, but that does not necessarily mean a return to v. (I think the "{}\+Berger\textquotesingle{}s"{} vector of physics is the displacement from the center of v to the center of the end vertex.). 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em v} & int \\
\hline
{\em w} & int, neighboring vertices, \\
\hline
{\em n} & int, n$>$=1, sidelength \\
\hline

\index{packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}!holonomyMobius@{holonomyMobius}}
\index{holonomyMobius@{holonomyMobius}!packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}}
\doxysubsubsection{holonomyMobius()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpacking_1_1_pack_data_a8d1f92c85f9181b5e0161c39a7697378} 
\textbf{ Mobius} packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+holonomy\+Mobius (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Pack\+Data}}]{p}{, }\item[{\textbf{ Half\+Link}}]{hlink}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Compute \doxyref{Mobius}{p.}{classmath_1_1_mobius} associated with holonomy along a closed chain of faces. The faces are defined by given \textquotesingle{}\doxyref{Half\+Link}{p.}{classlist_manip_1_1_half_link}\textquotesingle{}, the first assumed to be in the desired geometric location. Centers are then recomputed iteratively until the final locations of the original face vertices are found. Note that data in the packing is not changed. The transformation and its Frobenius norm (how close to identity) are displayed in \textquotesingle{}Messages\textquotesingle{} and written to a file if fp!=null. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p} & \doxyref{Pack\+Data}{p.}{classpacking_1_1_pack_data}, \\
\hline
{\em hlink} & \doxyref{Half\+Link}{p.}{classlist_manip_1_1_half_link} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxyref{Mobius}{p.}{classmath_1_1_mobius}, null on error 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}!label\_seed\_generations@{label\_seed\_generations}}
\index{label\_seed\_generations@{label\_seed\_generations}!packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}}
\doxysubsubsection{label\_seed\_generations()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpacking_1_1_pack_data_a302d5a0e7a1039c0ef28cce7a082ad01} 
int[$\,$] packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+label\+\_\+seed\+\_\+generations (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{seed}{, }\item[{int[$\,$]}]{greens}{, }\item[{int}]{max}{, }\item[{boolean}]{far}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Return array giving the generations of vertices from \textquotesingle{}seed\textquotesingle{}; (NOTE:\+ \textquotesingle{}util\+\_\+A\textquotesingle{} and \textquotesingle{}util\+\_\+B\textquotesingle{} are used to pass information back, calling routine must use these immediately on return.) Array \textquotesingle{}greens\textquotesingle{} must be either null or of length node\+Count+1; say vert v is "{}green"{} if greens[v]$<$0. (Typically, greens indicates circles already handled, eg., already in some other sub-\/complex.). 

Store generations from \textquotesingle{}seed\textquotesingle{} up to max, but stopping at green verts. If far is true, continue past max (if necessary) to first vert which is boundary or green; \textquotesingle{}util\+\_\+A\textquotesingle{} returns its index (otherwise, \textquotesingle{}util\+\_\+A\textquotesingle{} returns some vert of the largest generation reached) as a way to identify the "{}outside"{} of the max generation sub-\/complex. (Caution:\+ not all vertices will have an assigned generation in returned array.) Return \textquotesingle{}null\textquotesingle{} on error; return count via \textquotesingle{}util\+\_\+B\textquotesingle{} and \textquotesingle{}far\+\_\+vert\textquotesingle{} via \textquotesingle{}util\+\_\+A\textquotesingle{}. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em seed} & int, starting vertex \\
\hline
{\em greens} & int[], stop when greens $<$0 \\
\hline
{\em max} & int, stop here if max$>$0. \\
\hline
{\em far} & boolean \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
int[] containing generations. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}!path\_construct@{path\_construct}}
\index{path\_construct@{path\_construct}!packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}}
\doxysubsubsection{path\_construct()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpacking_1_1_pack_data_aeb5f232e88337ecfcae575bf1a8473e6} 
\textbf{ Node\+Link} packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+path\+\_\+construct (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{mode}{, }\item[{int}]{v1}{, }\item[{\textbf{ Node\+Link}}]{vertlist}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Return vertices defining an edge path proceeding from \textquotesingle{}v1\textquotesingle{} and taken from the given \textquotesingle{}vertlist\textquotesingle{}. Currently two methods:\+ 


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item flag=0:\+ multiple-\/choice (default:\+ for multi-\/sheeted surfaces):\+ return as many successive neighbors as possible.
\item flag=1:\+ return successive neighbors described in edge \textquotesingle{}turns\textquotesingle{} in combinatoric direction. First in vertlist must be a neighbor of v1, then succession of increments. E.\+g., "{}path\+\_\+c -\/i 23 57 2 4 0 3 3"{} will start with edge \{23,57\}, then \{57,x\}, where in the flower for 57, \{57,x\} is "{}2"{} edges counterclockwise from \{57,23\}, then "{}4"{} edges around x, then "{}0"{} (back up), etc. In a hex packing, "{}path\+\_\+c -\/i 23 57 3 3 3 ..."{} defines a combinatorial straight path. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mode} & int \\
\hline
{\em v1} & int \\
\hline
{\em vertlist} & \doxyref{Node\+Link}{p.}{classlist_manip_1_1_node_link} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxyref{Node\+Link}{p.}{classlist_manip_1_1_node_link} 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxyItemize}

\index{packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}!proj\_max\_to\_s@{proj\_max\_to\_s}}
\index{proj\_max\_to\_s@{proj\_max\_to\_s}!packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}}
\doxysubsubsection{proj\_max\_to\_s()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpacking_1_1_pack_data_a77c016cfe56211103aeb3cb530c33dc3} 
int packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+proj\+\_\+max\+\_\+to\+\_\+s (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{E}{, }\item[{double}]{ratio}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Project hyp max packing (already computed and laid out) to sphere with normalization options; combination of \textquotesingle{}geom\+\_\+to\+\_\+s\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}add\+\_\+ideal\textquotesingle{}, and \textquotesingle{}NSpole\textquotesingle{}. 

Use eucl intermediary for numerical reasons. Alpha vert goes to north pole, added ideal vertex S to south. If argument \textquotesingle{}E\textquotesingle{} is positive, then use it as east pole (so it gets centered at 1 on the sphere); else if \textquotesingle{}ratio\textquotesingle{} positive, then use as ratio of alpha/\+S; else ratio=1.\+0. Note:\+ if packing is hyperbolic, but bdry circles are not horocycles, then the spherical packing will not be coherent.

{\em ratio} & double \\
\hline

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpacking_1_1_pack_data_a6bf620422062f43656f14f987b901074} 
int packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+puncture\+\_\+face (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{f}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Remove a face, converting its three vertices to form a new 3-\/edge boundary component. \doxyref{Face}{p.}{classcombinatorics_1_1komplex_1_1_face} needs to be at least 2 generations distant from the original boundary to avoid disconnecting things. Geometry is not changed; local face list data is tossed. Calling routine does \textquotesingle{}complex\+\_\+count\textquotesingle{}, etc.

\index{packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}!right\_slide@{right\_slide}}
\index{right\_slide@{right\_slide}!packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}}
\doxysubsubsection{right\_slide()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpacking_1_1_pack_data_a24582ae884e436d92b1552aa3d8f2851} 
int packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+right\+\_\+slide (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Half\+Link}}]{hlink}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This is more general version of \textquotesingle{}hex\+\_\+slide\textquotesingle{} mechanism. Perform an edge flip on the edge to the right of each halfedge in \textquotesingle{}hlink\textquotesingle{}, i.\+e., flip twin.\+next. The effect when \textquotesingle{}hlink\textquotesingle{} is closed half-\/hex loop is to cut the packing along hlink and slide the right side one notch down before reattaching. Continue flipping as long as flips are successful, then fix the combinatorics.

int count, -\/count if there was a failure

int packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+scale\+\_\+rad (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Pack\+Data}}]{q}{, }\item[{double}]{x}{, }\item[{\textbf{ Node\+Link}}]{vertlist}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Reset radii of p to interpolate between current values and values in q by factor:\+ rad\+\_\+p(v)=rad\+\_\+p(v) + x$\ast$[rad\+\_\+p(v)-\/rad\+\_\+q(v)]. Infinite radii in hyperbolic are treated as value 10.\+0. Return count of adjustments.

\index{packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}!schFlowerErr@{schFlowerErr}}
\index{schFlowerErr@{schFlowerErr}!packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}}
\doxysubsubsection{schFlowerErr()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpacking_1_1_pack_data_aabd352d7cff420f967aec4ad26676c63} 
\textbf{ Pack\+Data} packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+sch\+Flower\+Err (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Vertex}}]{vert}{, }\item[{\textbf{ Complex}}]{err}{, }\item[{\textbf{ Circle\+Simple}}]{cs}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Generate a euclidean flower packing based on \textquotesingle{}vert\textquotesingle{} but using only its intrinsic schwarzians and recover the \textquotesingle{}error\textquotesingle{} in layout of the last petal. See \textquotesingle{}\doxyref{Pack\+Creation.\+seed}{p.}{classpacking_1_1_pack_creation_af1bd24fca1666865ca8d25f9d01a72d6}\textquotesingle{} for description. Comparing initial/\+final layouts of cn lead to the \textquotesingle{}err\textquotesingle{}=x+iy, where:\+ x = (newrad -\/ rad)/\+rad for cn y = (anglechange -\/ aim)/\+aim \textquotesingle{}cs\textquotesingle{} contains the new data for cn in case the user wants to use it.

{\em cs} & \doxyref{Circle\+Simple}{p.}{classgeometry_1_1_circle_simple}, instantiated by calling routine \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxyref{Pack\+Data}{p.}{classpacking_1_1_pack_data}, null for bdry vertex 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}!set\_single\_invDist@{set\_single\_invDist}}

\doxysubsubsection{set\_single\_invDist()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpacking_1_1_pack_data_a5d118aaa36cb1b255767c066864d994d} 
int packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+set\+\_\+single\+\_\+inv\+Dist (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{v}{, }\item[{int}]{w}{, }\item[{double}]{inv\+Dist}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Store one legal inversive distance value for edge and its twin. Note:\+ \textquotesingle{}inv\+Dist\textquotesingle{} values:\+ deep overlap in (-\/1,0); normal overlap in [0,1]; separated circles in (1,infty); tangency is 1. Note:\+ if \textquotesingle{}inv\+Dist\textquotesingle{} lies in [-\/1,1] then intersecting circles overlap with angle acos(inv\+Dist). If separated, \textquotesingle{}inv\+Dist\textquotesingle{} lies in [1,infty).

{\em w} & int \\
\hline
{\em inv\+Dist} & double, lies in [-\/1,infty) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

int, 1 on success 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{set\_xyz\_overlaps()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpacking_1_1_pack_data_ae6df65c581d26222374582a44728fb3e} 
int packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+set\+\_\+xyz\+\_\+overlaps (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Point3D}[$\,$]}]{xyz\+\_\+list}{, }\item[{int}]{flag}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Use xyz data to set \textquotesingle{}inv\+Dist\textquotesingle{}s. This command is still evolving. Eventually, may want to specify which ones to set; for now, set all. 

flag=1:\+ find max/\+min edge lengths in xyz data, set inv distances as though circle radii were all min/\+2.

flag=2:\+ for each vertex v find min edgelength, set inv distance as though radius of v is half that.

Radii are NOT changed --- only used to set inv\+Distances. Return count, 0 on error.

Store given radius \textquotesingle{}r\textquotesingle{} in internal form. Only issue is hyp case:\+ when r$>$8.\+0, treat as horocycle, when \textquotesingle{}r\textquotesingle{} is the actual hyperbolic radius, it is converted to x\+\_\+radius for storage. ~\newline
 For numerical reasons, small hyp radii \textquotesingle{}r\textquotesingle{} is converted to x=2$\ast$r$\ast$(2-\/r$\ast$(1-\/2$\ast$r/\+3)). (Recall x=1-\/exp(-\/2h)=1-\/s$^\wedge$2.).

\index{packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}!sq\_grid\_overlaps@{sq\_grid\_overlaps}}
\index{sq\_grid\_overlaps@{sq\_grid\_overlaps}!packing.PackData@{packing.PackData}}
\doxysubsubsection{sq\_grid\_overlaps()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpacking_1_1_pack_data_af753b8d6b705895563d69e3965d0e515} 
int packing.\+Pack\+Data.\+sq\+\_\+grid\+\_\+overlaps (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



"{}\+Square grid"{} packings typically have (interior) vertices of degrees 4 and 8, and the "{}ball bearings"{}, those of degree 4, have overlaps of angle pi/\+2 with their neighbors. This command simply sets pi/\+2 overlaps for all interior circles of degree 4 (whether packing has square grid combinatorics or not). 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
int count 
\end{DoxyReturn}
